The Language of Kǂūǂʢian

Natively known as: Kǂūǂʢ /kǂuːǂʢ/

...and he stood holding his hat and turned his wet face to the wind...
gæ il ʘʼaǂqī o kǁālungǁ ǁˀu gæ kǀxangʘī o ngʘad̀ī eǂq ingǁ yo
Pronunciation: /gæː il ˈʘʼɜǂqiː o ˈkǁaːluŋǁ ǁˀu gæː ˈkǀxɜŋʘiː o ˈŋʘɜɗiː eǂq iŋǁ jo/
Kǂūǂʢian word order: and stood holding his hat he and turned his wet face the wind to

Stress pattern: Initial — stress is on the first syllable

Word final consonants: d, j, k, kǀ, kǀx, kǁ, kǁx, kǂ, kǂx, kǃ, kǃx, kʘ, kʘx, l, m, n, p, r, w, z, ŋǀ, ŋǁ, ŋǂ, ŋʘ, ǀ, ǀq, ǀʢ, ǀʼ, ǀˀ, ǀχ, ǁ, ǁq, ǁʢ, ǁʼ, ǁˀ, ǁχ, ǂ, ǂq, ǂʢ, ǂʼ, ǂˀ, ǂχ, ǃ, ǃq, ǃʢ, ǃʼ, ǃˀ, ǃχ, ɓ, ɕ, ɗ, ʄ, ʑ, ʔ, ʘ, ʘq, ʘʢ, ʘʼ, ʘˀ, ʘχ

Phonological rules (in order of application):

  • N → ŋk / _V
  • e → i / _#
  • b → w / V_V
  • r → j / _#

Grammar

Main word order: Verb-Object-Oblique-Subject. "Mary opened the door with a key" turns into Opened the door with a key Mary.
Adjective order: Adjectives are positioned before the noun.
Adposition: postpositions

Noun

Singular Plural
Masculine No affix
ǃāp /ǃaːp/ 		Suffix -ekǁ
ǃāpekǁ /ˈǃaːpekǁ/
Feminine No affix
ǃāp /ǃaːp/ 		Suffix -iːǁ
ǃāpīǁ /ˈǃaːpiːǁ/
Neuter No affix
ǃāp /ǃaːp/ 		Suffix -oŋʘ
ǃāpongʘ /ˈǃaːpoŋʘ/

Nouns have seven cases:
Ergative is the doer of a verb: dog bites man
The ergative affix only appears if there is an absolutive in the sentence
Absolutive is the done-to of a verb: man bites dog
Absolutives are always no affix
Genitive is the possessor of something: dog’s tail hits man
Dative is the recipeint of something: man gives ball to dog
Locative is the location of something: man walks to town
Ablative is movement away from something: man walks from town
Instrumental is the use of something: man writes with (using) pen

Ergative Suffix -i

ǃāp /ǃaːp/
Genitive Suffix -aːl
ǃāpāl /ˈǃaːpaːl/
Dative If ends with vowel: Suffix -ǂq
Else: Suffix -iǂq
ǃāpiǂq /ˈǃaːpiǂq/
Locative If ends with vowel: Suffix -kǃxɜ
Else: Suffix -oːkǃxɜ
ǃāpōkǃxa /ˈǃaːpoːkǃxɜ/
Ablative If ends with vowel: Suffix -ǀʼ
Else: Suffix -oǀʼ
ǃāpoǀʼ /ˈǃaːpoǀʼ/
Instrumental If ends with vowel: Suffix -ǀˀu
Else: Suffix -uǀˀu
ǃāpuǀˀu /ˈǃaːpuǀˀu/

Articles

Kǂūǂʢian has no definite article ‘the’, or indefinite article ‘a’.

Verbs

Else: Suffix -uǂχ

ǂʼōʘxīʘ /ˈǂʼoːʘχiːʘ/

Derivational morphology

Adjective → noun = Suffix -æː
Noun → adjective = If ends with vowel: Suffix -ŋǁeː
Else: Suffix -iŋǁeː
Noun → verb = If ends with vowel: Suffix -nsi
Else: Suffix -insi
Verb → noun = If ends with vowel: Suffix -mpɜ
Else: Suffix -uːmpɜ
Verb → adjective = Suffix -aː
Adjective → verb = If ends with vowel: Suffix -ǀʼ
Else: Suffix -oǀʼ
Adjective → adverb = If ends with vowel: Suffix -ŋʘ
Else: Suffix -aːŋʘ
One who Xs (e.g. paint → painter) = If ends with vowel: Suffix -ǀ
Else: Suffix -uːǀ
Place of (e.g. wine → winery) = If ends with vowel: Suffix -ǁʢ
Else: Suffix -oːǁʢ
Diminutive = If ends with vowel: Suffix -buː
Else: Suffix -ubuː
Augmentative = If ends with vowel: Suffix -ǁχ
Else: Suffix -eǁχ
